## Model Usefulness Summary

- `hmm_v4_path_aware_meta` T+1: exact accuracy is lower than adjacent-tolerant accuracy, so most misses are neighboring-regime errors.
- `hmm_v4_path_aware_meta` T+1: missed-risk rate is elevated (52.1%); risk transitions may be under-warned.
